## Merkantilismus
##############################
theocracy_tier_2_wirt_1_1 = {
	icon = "idea_variation_28"	
	allow_normal_conversion = yes
	potential = {
		has_country_flag = iv_gov_reform_theo_tier_2_wirt
	}
	effect = {
	custom_tooltip = IV_REFORM_MERCANTILISM
	}
	valid_for_nation_designer = yes
	nation_designer_cost = 0
	modifiers = {
		trade_efficiency = -0.1
		embargo_efficiency = 0.5
		# <<WIKI>> decision = iv_mercanti_dec
	}

}
